## Diagram 3

```mermaid
graph LR
    A[status prop] --> B[parseExternalStatus]
    B --> C[mainStatus]
    C --> D[ExternalStateText Component]
    C --> E[ExternalState Component]
    D --> F[Text Component with color]
    E --> G[Styled div with background]
    F --> H[Display status text]
    G --> I[Display mainStatus badge]
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Evaluating
    Evaluating --> SHIPPABLE: Status is SHIPPABLE
    Evaluating --> NON_SHIPPABLE: Status is NON_SHIPPABLE
    Evaluating --> Other: Any other status
    SHIPPABLE --> GreenStyling
    NON_SHIPPABLE --> RedStyling
    Other --> GrayStyling
    GreenStyling --> Rendered
    RedStyling --> Rendered
    GrayStyling --> Rendered
    Rendered --> [*]
```
